  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f0d04e56-9d58-4d08-95a7-dd1ba6c10516'
      });

  <span id="freeText2159353732578684044" style="display:none">Moments.<br /><br />Our lives are a collection of moments. Some utterly painful and full of yesterday's hurts. Some beautifully hopeful and full of tomorrow's promises.<br /><br />I’ve had many moments in my lifetime, moments that changed me, challenged me. Moments that scared me and engulfed me. However, the biggest ones—the most heartbreaking and breathtaking ones—all included him.<br /><br />I was ten years old when I lost my voice. A piece of me was stolen away, and the only person who could truly hear my silence was Brooks Griffin. He was the light during my dark days, the promise of tomorrow, until tragedy found him. Tragedy that eventually drowned him in a sea of memories.<br /><br />This is the story of a boy and girl who loved each other, but didn’t love themselves. A story of life and death. Of love and broken promises.<br /><br />Of moments.<br /><br />(Book Three in the Elements Series. Complete Standalone. Coming Fall 2016.)</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1616864934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2721507371610163405"><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/DE154678-5BB8-46E8-AF55-C3F3EEFA84DA_zpsheg8lghz.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474275471i/20574863._SX540_.png' alt=' photo DE154678-5BB8-46E8-AF55-C3F3EEFA84DA_zpsheg8lghz.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist.”</blockquote>
</b> No one can write a book quite like Brittainy C. Cherry. Her stories are moving. Her story-telling abilities are off the charts amazing and her books are always epic for me. Whenever I start a new book by her, I just know it will be exceptionally good. <i>The Silent Waters</i> is my 5th book by Brittainy, and I have to say- I think it’s my favorite one so far. That is a HUGE deal because she has written some of my favorite books ever. Whe</span>
  <span id="freeText2721507371610163405" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/DE154678-5BB8-46E8-AF55-C3F3EEFA84DA_zpsheg8lghz.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474275471i/20574863._SX540_.png" alt=" photo DE154678-5BB8-46E8-AF55-C3F3EEFA84DA_zpsheg8lghz.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>“The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist.”</blockquote>
</b> No one can write a book quite like Brittainy C. Cherry. Her stories are moving. Her story-telling abilities are off the charts amazing and her books are always epic for me. Whenever I start a new book by her, I just know it will be exceptionally good. <i>The Silent Waters</i> is my 5th book by Brittainy, and I have to say- I think it’s my favorite one so far. That is a HUGE deal because she has written some of my favorite books ever. When you start this book, be prepared to be feel, to love, to be inspired, to have an unforgettable story engraved on your soul. And I’ll repeat <b>BE PREPARED TO FEEL</b>. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/6C0E2063-7D21-4AC3-9B8C-C8DE0AE0B6BA_zpskkrfuyr4.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474275471i/20574864._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 6C0E2063-7D21-4AC3-9B8C-C8DE0AE0B6BA_zpskkrfuyr4.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Moments.</b> When it comes down to it, that’s what all our lives are made of. A collection of moments. And a single moment can forever change your life… <i>The Silent Waters</i> is the story of Maggie Riley and Brooks Griffin’s moments. All the important moments in their lives, the other was a part of. It started when they were kids. A childhood romance turned into a lifelong friendship, turned into so much more. <br><br>Oh, my. The things I could say about this story. The things I want to say about this story. But you know what the best part of this story is? The way you will FEEL when reading. I don’t want to take that experience away from anyone so the actual story… yeah. Not talking about it at all. My lips are sealed. Experience the book. Feel the story. I am a reader who reads to feel. All of my favorite books have this in common- they have strong emotion and really dig deep and make me feel so much. This story has that quality in spades. Even though I’m not going to speak about the story, I will talk about the characters some. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/33FF60E0-719B-4671-AB6C-201E3F1FA8CB_zpsd6rwiaad.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474275471i/20574865._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 33FF60E0-719B-4671-AB6C-201E3F1FA8CB_zpsd6rwiaad.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maggie Mae Riley is a special person. And so is Brooks Tyler Griffin. Maggie is someone I liked from the moment I met her. The more time I spent with her, the more I liked her. I felt for her. I understood her. Brooks and Maggie are two characters that belong together. I truly believe that. Brooks is a pretty incredible hero. One of my favorite things about a B Cherry book is that ALL of her characters are wonderful, not just the main ones. They all have a purpose to the story and depth to them. Maggie’s father, Cheryl, Mrs. Boone, Calvin, Katie, the list could go on and on. They are all great in their own right. Even the ones that I hated for a moment or two. Even the ones the frustrated me at times. I still loved them all. <br><br>In this story, there are heartbreaking moments. There are moments my heart soared. Moments that tore me apart, and moments that pieced me back together. Every moment of this book was special. Every single moment had an impact on me. <br><br>When I read a book by B. Cherry, I know it won’t be the same old same old romance story. I know it will be special. I know it will be beautiful. I know it will speak to my heart. Brittainy is one of the only authors that has that quality for me. No matter what she writes, it touches my soul and hits every single one of my love buttons. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/32226090-9A31-4F2D-99ED-51C0D600B783_zpsmlprzy29.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474275471i/20574866._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 32226090-9A31-4F2D-99ED-51C0D600B783_zpsmlprzy29.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Five minutes?” Five minutes. We stood there, staring at one another. Five minutes to erase any fears. Five minutes to remember who we were. Five minutes to find our own way, our own story. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>This is a book that will stay with you. I can say with absolute certainty I will never forget reading this book. I will never forget the characters, I will never forget the words, and I will never forget how I felt when I read it. The tears that streamed down my face during those moments in the story… It’s a tale that will stay forever etched on my heart. <br><br><i>The Silent Waters</i> is a truly exceptional read. Brittainy’s words are magical and the story was perfect for me. Don’t be surprised if you see this at #1 on my 2016 favorites list. I give it all the stars! <br><i>
  <blockquote>Sometimes the rain was more pleasing than the sun. Sometimes the hurt was more fulfilling than the healing. And sometimes the pieces of the puzzle were more beautiful when scattered apart.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/E0B4499A-EF7E-409A-8822-1FA2CD52EF9A_zpsbps7wzei.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474275471i/20574867._SX540_.png" alt=" photo E0B4499A-EF7E-409A-8822-1FA2CD52EF9A_zpsbps7wzei.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2721507371610163405" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1616643397" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1616643397" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1616643397?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1616643397" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2943653834761513939"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473129427i/20412927.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474992596i/20667121.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>'The Silent Waters'</i> is another wonderfully written story by Brittainy C. Cherry that I totally fell in love with. This author never ceases to amaze me with her amount of talent she possesses, with her amazing storytelling or with her unforgettable love stories that always are so unforgettable. This third book in the series was emotional, powerful, though-provoking, intense and like the other stories I’ve read by this author it made me feel so much. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474387425i/20592725.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The world keeps spinning because your </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText2943653834761513939" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473129427i/20412927.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474992596i/20667121.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>'The Silent Waters'</i> is another wonderfully written story by Brittainy C. Cherry that I totally fell in love with. This author never ceases to amaze me with her amount of talent she possesses, with her amazing storytelling or with her unforgettable love stories that always are so unforgettable. This third book in the series was emotional, powerful, though-provoking, intense and like the other stories I’ve read by this author it made me feel so much. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474387425i/20592725.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Maggie’s life changes completely when her single father meets Katie. Practically over the night Maggie seems to have everything a little girl wants and needs – a caring mother, a beautiful home and two new siblings she’s eager to know better. From the moment little Maggie meets Brooks, his new brother’ best friend, she’s smitten beyond words. Even if Maggie is just a little girl she knows he’s IT for her and she knows that someday he will become her groom. Years later when Maggie is just then years old something tragic happens. She loses herself, she loses her voice, a piece of her being stolen from her forever. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I hadn’t known you could hear someone’s voice so clearly in the silent moments.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Maggie has a hard time moving on with her life. From that night that changes her life irrevocably, Maggie in some way stops living. She lives in silence, her pain and her demons being too much at times. The only one who seems to hear her, to hear her silence being her anchor over the years is Brooks, the boy who wants nothing more to fix the girl who means so much to him, the boy who constantly remembers her that she matters, that her voice matters. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“With each touch, I fell more for his spirit. With each kiss, I tasted a part of his soul.<br> 	In my mind, I whispered back to him, time and time again. With every tear and every heartbeat, I spoke to him. So quiet, yet so loud.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474387425i/20592728.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>'The Silent Waters'</i> was a fantastic read from beginning until the end and it touched me more than I can say. Maggie and Brooks’s journey to happiness was intense, tumultuous and not very easy to read at times. However, I enjoyed it very much. I enjoyed every minute of it and I honestly experienced everything these two characters experienced as the story unfolded. Their love story was epic, beautiful and it made me feel so much. <br><br>I loved Maggie and Brooks individually and I loved them together. These characters were wonderful developed and so endearing. I liked Maggie’s character from the moment she was introduced. I liked her as a little girl and I liked her as a woman. My heart broke for her and for how much she lost over the years. Her pain, her fears, her insecurities were wonderful portrayed. I felt them all as the story progressed, but I also felt her love for her family, her love for music and books and her love for Brooks. Her voice was powerful through the pages even if she didn’t have a voice and the chapters written from her point-of-view were honestly so hard to read at times, so emotional. <br><br>Brooks was as amazing hero. He was sweet, caring, thoughtful, considerate and so much more. I don't have enough words to tell you how much I loved his character. But what I loved the most was the way he loved Maggie -unconditionally, how over the years he became her anchor, how he never gave up on her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Five minutes?” Five minutes. We stood there, staring at one another. Five minutes to erase any fears. Five minutes to remember who we were. Five minutes to find our own way, our own story.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Maggie and Brooks’s friendship was beautiful. I simply loved the way they were with each other – their honesty, how easily they communicate with each other and I honestly loved all the sweet, heartwarming, but also heartbreaking moments between them. I never doubted these two characters are meant to be together because I felt how much they loved each other more and more with every single chapter. <br><br>As always, Brittainy C. Cherry’s supporting characters were fantastically portrayed and endearing in some way or another. All of them played a role in Maggie and Brooks’s story and all of them had so much depth. The supporting character I loved the most was Maggie’s father. The relationship between Maggie and her father was pure and simple wonderful. He was such a great father, so loving and so caring. I have to mention the author’s note in the end. It was short, simple, yet so powerful. Make sure you read it as soon as you finish Maggie and Brooks's story. <br><br>All in all, <i>'The Silent Waters'</i> was another wonderful story by Brittainy C. Cherry. It was beautiful, it was special and it will make you feel so much from the beginning until the end. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She was right about me, and her, and us. She’d be the one girl I’d love forever. No matter how life tried to change us."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474387425i/20592729.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Find me on:</b><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525702.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525703.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.steamyreads.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525705.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1767895475" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1767895475" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1767895475?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32070295-the-silent-waters">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rock-stars">rock-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1767895475" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16480275098110044256">Check out more of my reviews at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.bookaddicthaven.com'>www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br/><br/>I've now read several of Brittainy C. Cherry's books and she never ceases to amaze me with how emotional and heartfelt her stories are. I know that when I pick up one of her books I am going to be a mess before it is over. She breaks my heart into tiny pieces and then slowly puts me back together from the wreckage. It's a very love/hate relationship that I have with her work.<br/><br/>'The Silent Waters' was no exception. I fell in love with the chara</span>
  <span id="freeText16480275098110044256" style="display:none">Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br /><br />I've now read several of Brittainy C. Cherry's books and she never ceases to amaze me with how emotional and heartfelt her stories are. I know that when I pick up one of her books I am going to be a mess before it is over. She breaks my heart into tiny pieces and then slowly puts me back together from the wreckage. It's a very love/hate relationship that I have with her work.<br /><br />'The Silent Waters' was no exception. I fell in love with the characters and the beautiful, yet tragic, story. It made me fall in love. It gutted me. It broke my heart. It gave me hope. This is one book that will take you on an emotional rollercoaster ride.<br /><br />We first meet Maggie as a young girl. Her father has remarried and she moves into her new home with her new family. Early on, she attaches herself to her slightly older step-brother and his best-friend, Brooks. She is the cute little girl that tags along everywhere that they go, crushing on Brooks and planning their wedding. <br /><br />Initially, Brooks is irritated by Maggie and her girlish crush, until they kiss one day. From that point forward, the two are inseparable. Brooks and Maggie are the quintessential picture of childhood love.<br /><br />On the day that Maggie and Brooks are supposed to have their "wedding" in the forest Brooks is late. A ten year-old Maggie goes into the forest that day, but is never the same again. What happened in the forest leaves her traumatized and her fear imprisons her.<br /><br />The events of that day will have a ripple effect on everyone in Maggie's life. Guilt and "what-ifs" slowly eat away at the people Maggie cares about the most, damaging relationships and fostering resentment. Yet, Brooks' dedication to her is steadfast.<br /><br />Over the years, life takes different characters down different paths. The dynamics of relationships change. Some grow stronger, some fade away. Old ghosts still linger, until the truth comes out so many years later.<br /><br />I am being intentionally vague, because I don't want to spoil this beautiful story for anyone. This is a book that should be experienced. It is sentimental and emotional, but so worth it. I highly recommend this book to anyone looking for a heartfelt, well-developed, slow-burn romance. This story is fantastic! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16480275098110044256" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15314619830660323611"><b>2.5 Stars</b><br/><br/> I’m not going to lie, I feel terrible.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474911654i/20655865._SY540_.jpg' width='300"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>First of all, I would like to point out three things:<br/><br/><b>1.</b> Brittainy C. Cherry is my <b>
  <i>favorite</i>
</b> author. I’ve read all of her books and I loved them all. Well, all except this one.<br/><br/><b>2.</b> I still believe Brittainy C. Cherry is one of the <b>
  <i>most talented</i>
</b> contemporary romance authors.<br/><br/><b>3.</b> Since I bought and read this book, I feel kind of entitled to express <b>
  <i>my personal feelings</i>
</b> freely and openly.<br/><br/>This book started off beautifully and I loved every secon</span>
  <span id="freeText15314619830660323611" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars</b><br><br> I’m not going to lie, I feel terrible.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474911654i/20655865._SY540_.jpg" width='300"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>First of all, I would like to point out three things:<br><br><b>1.</b> Brittainy C. Cherry is my <b>
  <i>favorite</i>
</b> author. I’ve read all of her books and I loved them all. Well, all except this one.<br><br><b>2.</b> I still believe Brittainy C. Cherry is one of the <b>
  <i>most talented</i>
</b> contemporary romance authors.<br><br><b>3.</b> Since I bought and read this book, I feel kind of entitled to express <b>
  <i>my personal feelings</i>
</b> freely and openly.<br><br>This book started off beautifully and I loved every second of it. Right until the tragic event. After that everything went downhill for me.<br><br><b>Reasons?</b><br><br><b>1.</b> I had a problem with the <i>
  <b>plot</b>
</i>. The whole situation with the heroine pissed me off. I felt like everybody around her accepted her illness/trauma too easily and took it for granted. I think her parents didn’t do enough. I don’t understand why her loving and educated father, a university professor no less, didn’t try harder. Maybe the whole thing could have been avoided?<br><br><b>2.</b> <b>
  <i>My feelings</i>
</b>. This book is beautifully written. Although being tragic and profound, at times it felt too sappy and cheesy to me, borderline unbelievable. I missed that rawness, grittiness and realness that can be found in this author’s previous books. I simply couldn’t relate to the characters or the story. <br><br><b>3.</b> The <b>
  <i>flow of the story</i>
</b>. The leaps from one period to another felt too sudden and sharp. The ending felt a little bit implausible. Is it possible (from the medical point of view) for a person to start speaking again just like that after such a long period? Also, some parts of this book were really frustrating and boring for me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474911654i/20655870.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Despite the above reasons, I feel like I should stress that the writing and the characterization are great. <br><br>If you haven’t read this book yet, do it. Brittainy C. Cherry is an amazing writer. A lot of readers loved this book, maybe I just chose to read it at the wrong time.<br><br><b>QUICK REVIEW:</b><br><br><b>Enjoyment:</b>: 2.5/5<br><b>Writing style:</b> 5/5<br><b>Storyline:</b> 3/5<br><b>Hero:</b> 4/5<br><b>Heroine:</b> 3/5<br><b>Secondary characters:</b> 5/5 <br><b>Hotness/chemistry:</b> 2/5 <br><b>Romance:</b> 4/5 <br><b>Angst:</b> 4/5<br><b>Darkness level:</b> 3/5<br><b>Humor:</b> 3/5<br><b> Depth of the book:</b> 4/5<br><b>POV:</b> dual, 1st person<br><b> Triggers:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[murder, PTSD  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4180425806485105460">~*~Official Blurb for The Silent Waters~*~<br/><br/>Moments.<br/><br/>Our lives are a collection of moments. Some utterly painful and full of yesterday's hurts. Some beautifully hopeful and full of tomorrow's promise.<br/><br/>I’ve had many moments in my lifetime, moments that changed me, challenged me. Moments that scared me and engulfed me. However, the biggest ones—the most heartbreaking and breathtaking ones—all included him.<br/><br/>I was eight-years-old when I lost my voice. A piece of me was stolen away, and the only person wh</span>
  <span id="freeText4180425806485105460" style="display:none">~*~Official Blurb for The Silent Waters~*~<br /><br />Moments.<br /><br />Our lives are a collection of moments. Some utterly painful and full of yesterday's hurts. Some beautifully hopeful and full of tomorrow's promise.<br /><br />I’ve had many moments in my lifetime, moments that changed me, challenged me. Moments that scared me and engulfed me. However, the biggest ones—the most heartbreaking and breathtaking ones—all included him.<br /><br />I was eight-years-old when I lost my voice. A piece of me was stolen away, and the only person who could truly hear my silence was Brooks Griffin. He was the light during my dark days, the promise of tomorrow, until tragedy found him. Tragedy that eventually drowned him in a sea of memories.<br /><br />This is the story of a boy and girl who loved each other, but didn’t love themselves. A story of life and death. Of love and broken promises.<br /><br />Of moments.</span>

<div id="review_1746590137" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1746590137" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1746590137?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=not-sure-any-book-can-ever-top-this">not-sure-any-book-can-ever-top-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=utterly-heartbreaking">utterly-heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=second-chance-love">second-chance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s">books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1746590137" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4542585708540435991"><b>*****FIVE+++++++++++++++ STARS*****</b><br/>{ARC Generously Provided by Author}<br/>(BR with Mel and Dee)<br/><br/><br/><b>In that moment, I knew she had been right about everything all along. She was right about me, and her, and us. She’d be the one girl I’d love until forever. No matter how life tried to change us.”</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/8bd2b9afb1cd0601166fd6f4e7c58a0b_zps5cgmwvcd.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474556589i/20615989._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 8bd2b9afb1cd0601166fd6f4e7c58a0b_zps5cgmwvcd.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Just reading that one of so many quotes I loved in this book, gave me the chills. <b>THE SILENT WATERS</b> is nothing short of a <b>MASTERPIECE</b>. If you’ve ever read anything by Brittainy C Cherry, then you are already a</span>
  <span id="freeText4542585708540435991" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE+++++++++++++++ STARS*****</b><br>{ARC Generously Provided by Author}<br>(BR with Mel and Dee)<br><br><br><b>In that moment, I knew she had been right about everything all along. She was right about me, and her, and us. She’d be the one girl I’d love until forever. No matter how life tried to change us.”</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/8bd2b9afb1cd0601166fd6f4e7c58a0b_zps5cgmwvcd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474556589i/20615989._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8bd2b9afb1cd0601166fd6f4e7c58a0b_zps5cgmwvcd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Just reading that one of so many quotes I loved in this book, gave me the chills. <b>THE SILENT WATERS</b> is nothing short of a <b>MASTERPIECE</b>. If you’ve ever read anything by Brittainy C Cherry, then you are already aware of the amazing gift this woman has for storytelling. It was apparent from the very beginning of this book that it had the makings to be one of the <b>”Best of 2016”!!!</b> The author is going to make you experience a gamut of emotions during this journey with Maggie May and Brooks. Having read several of Brittainy’s books in the past, my heart was prepared for an emotional rollercoaster ride and I was more than ready to take the plunge! <br><br><br><br>Maggie May and Brooks Tyler have been childhood friends ever since she moved to Wisconsin with her father who had recently married a woman with two kids of her own. The cute letters back and forth between young Maggie and Brooks had me laughing so hard that my tummy ached. Oh but the laughter soon will die along with the adorable and exuberant voice of little Maggie May. Fast forward a few years, a ten-year-old Maggie has plans to wed her one and only true love, Brooks, out in the woods on the outskirts of their neighborhood. It is in these woods that Maggie goes through a traumatic experience that leaves a devastating psychological effect on her. Maggie has lost her ability to speak. But even through her darkest of times, there is a bright shining light that brings joy to her life in the form of a beautiful boy—Brooks!<br><br><br>Brooks' and Maggie May’s friendship was very much the pinnacle of the story for me. Even though Maggie has lost her ability to express herself vocally, the two communicate as if they were two halves of a whole. Their love of music and reading deepens the bond between them and during some particularly trying times it also soothes them. I fell so hard for Brooks. It is virtually impossible not to. His love for Maggie May knows no bounds, and really how could you not love a guy who would read his girl’s favorite books and then mail them to her with tons of post-it notes with his thoughts included??!! Seriously swoon-worthy to the millionth degree!!<br><br><br><br>There are several amazing secondary characters, one who deserves special mention is Mrs. Boone. The feisty old lady and Maggie have a truly special friendship. I got a kick out of her snarky attitude. What I love about this story is that it made me realize that I am too quick to judge people for their faults. There were a couple of characters that I immediately despised and I was not even willing to question what might be causing them to act out the way that they were. As the story develops we learn what drove those characters’ actions and it enabled me to forgive them. <br><br><br><br>This story is hard at times to endure and it had me bawling my eyes out one minute and then screaming in frustration the next. My advice to those of you who have not read this yet is to have a friend buddy read it with you. You are going to need someone to talk you down from throwing your kindle or iPAD across the room!! That is another thing that makes this story so fantastic – it really turned me into an emotional wreck. I felt so passionate about these characters and the heartbreak that transpires almost annihilated me!!<br><br><br><br>Do yourselves a favor and don’t wait even a minute to one-click and start reading this beautiful story! Whether or not you are a Brittainy C Cherry fan, I honestly don’t think you will be disappointed with this book!! For me, <b>THE SILENT WATERS</b> is going to be categorized as <b>THE BEST BOOK OF ALL TIME</b>!! It is one I will surely be re-reading over and over again for many years to come. <br><br><br><br>Make sure you read the author’s note at the end. If you didn’t love her before, that note will definitely turn you into an instant fangirl. I have even more respect for this amazing woman.<br><br><br><br>US: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2cIZzKM">http://amzn.to/2cIZzKM</a> <br>UK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2cJ0bAj">http://amzn.to/2cJ0bAj</a><br><br><br><br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452041283i/17638294.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1642973797?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=audio-listen">audio-listen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=rockstars-musicians">rockstars-musicians</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=arc-edelweiss-netgalley">arc-edelweiss-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1642973797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11860372042919380009"><b>NOW LIVE!</b><br/>*<a href='http://amzn.to/2jtJOHc' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a>*<a href='http://amzn.to/2cJ0bAj' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a>*<br/><br/><i>♫Audible listened to for a re-read 11/30/17♫</i><br/><br/><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/>This book quickly became my favorite by Brittainy C. Cherry and I just want to forget all about reading it so that I can read it again and experience it all as if it's the first time. It's definitely the kind of book that will stick with me for years to come. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382554981ra/5984941.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Brittainy wrote this story in such a way that it was as if she was speaking directly to me and telling me this beautifully heartbreaking story. This book was</span>
  <span id="freeText11860372042919380009" style="display:none"><b>NOW LIVE!</b><br>*<a href="http://amzn.to/2jtJOHc" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a>*<a href="http://amzn.to/2cJ0bAj" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a>*<br><br><i>♫Audible listened to for a re-read 11/30/17♫</i><br><br><b>4.5 Stars</b><br>This book quickly became my favorite by Brittainy C. Cherry and I just want to forget all about reading it so that I can read it again and experience it all as if it's the first time. It's definitely the kind of book that will stick with me for years to come. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382554981ra/5984941.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brittainy wrote this story in such a way that it was as if she was speaking directly to me and telling me this beautifully heartbreaking story. This book was extra special from her and it honestly felt like she had somehow found out my deepest thoughts and put them into this story. Sounds crazy, but I honestly thinks that's how most people will feel once they read this. <br><br>I easily immersed myself into the world of Maggie and Brooks, and silence. You know when you read a book and the characters emotions become yours, and it's like you become them. That's how this book was for me. I didn't speak the entire time I was reading it, I didn't even listen to music which is a big deal because I have music playing at every possible second. I just read this incredible story of hurt, and loss, and guilt, and fear and felt everything along with these characters. I don't even think I have the words to describe how much I loved the journey Brooks and Maggie took me on honestly. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474466854i/20603594._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brooks and Maggie had the kind of love that lasted through the pain, the tears, and the the moment that defines us all. I'm not talking about the happiest day of your life. I'm talking about the worst one, the day that broke us as humans, tore us apart and laughed in our face when we tried to put ourselves back together. That is the moment that will define you based on how you react to it. Brooks and Maggie had their moments years apart, and they both reacted differently to them, but the thing that didn't change was that they were there for one another. That is what made them the perfect couple. <br><br>I wanted to give this book five stars, I really really did. But there were parts in the beginning that had a little too much immaturity for me and it got to be a tad annoying, which is where the .5 got taken from my 5 star rating. Even with those times, though, I never stopped loving the characters.<br><br>I could probably go on and rant for even longer than I already have, but I'll stop here and just let you know that this is not a book you want to miss out on. It's something special and it needs to be read. <br><br><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15828952552974840999">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars</b> ★★★★★<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474290154i/20577926._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>It's been a while since I have been moved by a book as much as this one, I spent a good portion of my Saturday night crying, and the emotions that I felt whilst reading The Silent Waters were very intense and real.<br/><br/>Such a beautiful story of two childhood friends who love each other deeply, but where the timing is never quite right, and the circumstances of their lives keep them from achieving true happiness.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"I need you to know that even if you decide to never speak again, yo</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15828952552974840999" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars</b> ★★★★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474290154i/20577926._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It's been a while since I have been moved by a book as much as this one, I spent a good portion of my Saturday night crying, and the emotions that I felt whilst reading The Silent Waters were very intense and real.<br><br>Such a beautiful story of two childhood friends who love each other deeply, but where the timing is never quite right, and the circumstances of their lives keep them from achieving true happiness.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I need you to know that even if you decide to never speak again, you’ll always have someone around to hear you, Maggie. All right? I’ll always be there to listen to your silence."</b>
</blockquote><br>Maggie Riley and Brooks Griffin's story touched me so deeply, their journey is not an easy one, but the pain and the tears are outweighed by their wonderful friendship and their amazing moments together, and there were so many beautiful moments.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474289541i/20577861._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maggie is an intelligent and loving woman, who is crippled by fear. She is surrounded by love, her father, her step-siblings, her step-mother, Brooks, they all love her, but nobody can help her to overcome her greatest worries, they can only do their best and be there for her and give her strength by being a strong family unit.<br><br>Brooks is Maggie's brothers' bandmate, and vows to always be there for her, sharing his love of music with her, whilst she shares with him her of books.<br><br>Brittainy Cherry has the ability to really pull me into a story, I felt like I was living it, and even though it hurt, the painful parts were what made the good parts sweeter. I could not put this book down, and I urge anyone who loves to read an epic love story that puts you through the paces, to pick up this truly inspiring book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You have a voice, Maggie May. You always have. Now it’s just time for the rest of the world to hear it. "</b>
</blockquote><br>Straight onto the Top 2016 shelf...I simply loved it &lt;3<br><br><b>The Silent Waters is a standalone contemporary romance, told from dual POV's<b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received <div id="review_1617483399" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1617483399" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1617483399?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1617483399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16292208642748720674"><b> 4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”I loved how he could see me when the rest of the world forgot I existed.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Brittainy C. Cherry delivers yet another novel that will tug at your emotions the entire read. With her unique and endearing sense of humor, truly unforgettable quotes, and heart racing plot, this book made for a <s>good</s> great read. The heroine and hero are introduced as young children and their banter was fabulous!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Maggie May makes me sick. The thought of her gives me nightmares.” <br/><br/>“You say that </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText16292208642748720674" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”I loved how he could see me when the rest of the world forgot I existed.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Brittainy C. Cherry delivers yet another novel that will tug at your emotions the entire read. With her unique and endearing sense of humor, truly unforgettable quotes, and heart racing plot, this book made for a <s>good</s> great read. The heroine and hero are introduced as young children and their banter was fabulous!<br><br><b>
  <i>”Maggie May makes me sick. The thought of her gives me nightmares.” <br><br>“You say that because you love her,” Jamie mocked me.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1571265631ra/28304976.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Brooks Griffin’s childhood marriage proposals from Maggie Riley are so ADORABLE! The flow of the story is great and I was smiling happily when all of the sudden all the characters and a reader will be left sideswiped. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491916556ra/22461419.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Our once bubbly, carefree, confident, heroine has now become a shut-in and a mute ever since the events of one night. As time goes on and her family grows she remains with her novels (loved all the book references) and Brooks as her anchor.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I’ll be your anchor. I’ll help you stay grounded when you feel like you’re drifting away.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491916556ra/22461416.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br>The story is told in three parts as the characters grow the story spans years. I do wonder with the amount of therapy and concern that her family shows does Maggie not even discuss the events ever? Not even journaling? Just what did therapy consist of? I have to admit I got VERY antsy waiting for the heroine to address her situation instead of letting it run her. Has Bob not taught us anything?<br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>Anyway, years go by as Brooks is still tethered to Maggie and her to him, yet things are happening for his band and so she makes some big decisions. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Tell me to stay, and I’ll stay,” he begged. “Tell me to go, and I’ll go, but don’t keep me here in limbo, Maggie May. Don’t let me leave, not knowing. Don’t make me swim in unknown waters, because I’m certain the unknown is where I’ll drown.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491916556ra/22461420.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story takes some twists and turns with some good reveals as a reader hopes that Maggie will find her voice and be strong enough to step outside. The secondary characters in this story were terrific. I must give a shout out to her father, her stepsiblings, and of course Mrs. Boone!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461530619ra/18877927.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The writing is wonderful and the story very sweet yet I have to implore readers to read “A Note from the Author” because that was one kick ass piece of writing. That was so heartfelt and real and that for me should have been this story just expanded. Hoping in the future as a mother of a child who has faced bullying and a speech impediment that Brittainy make’s it happen! <br><br><b>
  <i>”She was right about me, and her, and us. She’d be the one girl I’d love forever. No matter how life tried to change us.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491916556ra/22461418.gif" width="430" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>
  <a data-text-id="16292208642748720674" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1616297575?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1616297575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14013887896197206211"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> The Silent Waters<br/><b>Series:</b> Elements #3<br/><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C. Cherry<br/><b>Release date: </b> September 22, 2016<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b>HEA</b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474299805i/20579413._SX540_.jpg' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There are very few times throughout the year I can say that I have a book hangover, and that's what this book has me nursing right now. I have a pile of ARCs to start reading, and I just can't move past this hauntingly beautiful story. These characters are truly a feast for every starving reader out there. They satisfy that craving for a book </span>
  <span id="freeText14013887896197206211" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> The Silent Waters<br><b>Series:</b> Elements #3<br><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C. Cherry<br><b>Release date: </b> September 22, 2016<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b>HEA</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474299805i/20579413._SX540_.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are very few times throughout the year I can say that I have a book hangover, and that's what this book has me nursing right now. I have a pile of ARCs to start reading, and I just can't move past this hauntingly beautiful story. These characters are truly a feast for every starving reader out there. They satisfy that craving for a book that will bring you to your knees. <br><br>Tall words, I know. <br>But truth, nonetheless.<br><br>Powerful, impactful, memorable. <i>That</i> is what you get with The Silent Waters. You slip into this book's shores gently, and get covered in a wave of emotion before you can blink. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474300921ra/20579497.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maggie and her father are drifting after her mother leaves, never staying in one place too long. But when he meets Katie everything changes. They have a new home, a new family, and a chance at happiness again. She settles into her life there and flourishes. As a child, Maggie has a light about her that shines and blinds everyone in her path. Most of all, her father. They have the type of relationship and bond that will melt you into a gooey puddle. The unconditional love that they have between them was absolutely beautiful. It not only grew in the happier times, but held solid in the darker days. They made my heart so happy.<br><br><b>"The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist." He'd said those words to me every single day, as long as I could remember.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474303298ra/20579833.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brooks is her brother's Calvin's best friend and though he tries to hate her, her charm was irresistible. The beginning of their story is just about the cutest thing I've read. Their letters to one another made me feel warm all over, and I fell so easily into how they begin to connect.<br><br>One moment in ten-year old Maggie's day is the turning point in her life. Her bright light is dimmed and nothing will ever be the same again.<br><br><i>Shh....</i><br><br><b>Maybe I'd fallen so deep into the back of my mind that I'd never have to remember what it was like to feel, to hurt, to break, to breathe.</b><br><br>Maggie's pain and inner demons will cut you deep. Her daily battle to fight back the fear and anxiety that plagues her is difficult enough. But the effects on everyone around her are large and staggering. Like a fissure in the strong foundation of their family, they slowly started to crack under the strain. One constant through it all, through all the aches of her struggle was Brooks. His ability to listen to her, to hear her without words became her comfort and her home. Sharing their love of music and books together, they become inseparable and their time together treasured. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474306685i/20580326.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Evolving past friendship wasn't the choice you would imagine. It just was. It was a realization more than a choice, these two people accepting what they were. They slipped easily into passion, and Brooks and Maggie were everything you could ask for. But time moves on, and Maggie is frozen in place. <br><br>I've never read a story like this. One that will make you hurt and happy, then fearful and excited at the same time. My emotions were turning in every direction, leaving me feeling wrung out and limp. Turning the pages becoming like a traumatic relief. You want her to conquer everything that imprisons her, what she holds inside so silently.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474308033ra/20580528.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>In my mind, I whispered back to him, time and time again. With every tear and every heartbeat, I spoke to him. So quiet, yet so loud.<br><i>I love you, too. I love you, too. I love you too...</i></b><br><br>Maggie and Brooks have a love story that's not simple or easy, nor is it convenient. But it's patient, and gentle, and everything right about falling for someone who fits you completely in every corner of yourself. I always come away from a Brittany C. Cherry book feeling overwhelmed with the enormity of what she expresses in her stories. How she manages to wreck you so painfully but make the end point of the journey so unforgettably good never ceases to amaze me. <br><br>I have high standards when it comes to this author because I know what she can deliver and once again she came through with flying colors. In fact, this is probably sitting in the top spot now as my favorite book by her, which is really saying something. Now if you'll excuse me, I'm going to go shout from the rooftops now to anyone who will listen to give this book a chance. <br><br><b>"It's not fair, you know, because every time I tried to move on your love kept pulling me back."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474309918ra/20580709.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" <div id="review_1760098859" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1760098859" />
    <a title="Bibi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33411728-bibi"><img alt="Bibi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602128191p2/33411728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1760098859?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bibi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bibi" href="/user/show/33411728-bibi">Bibi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1760098859" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8437000627914509467"><blockquote><b> *Spoilers*<br/><br/>Unintentionally, I fell into <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32294951.The_Gravity_of_Us__Elements___4_' title='The Gravity of Us (Elements, #4) by Brittainy C. Cherry' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Gravity of Us</a> (a brilliant book, btw) and with the warm fuzzies still swirling in my heart, I sought out other books by BC. <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29963453.The_Silent_Waters__Elements___3_' title='The Silent Waters (Elements, #3) by Brittainy C. Cherry' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Silent Waters</a> came up with glowing reviews, so, I hopped onto the train. Part one was too funny for words with both protagonists, Maggie and Brooks, meeting and engaging with each other as very young kids. Too cute.</b><br/><br/>The book takes a dark turn when Maggie witnesses and endures a terrible tragedy. A tragedy which impacted, for 18</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8437000627914509467" style="display:none"><blockquote><b> *Spoilers*<br /><br />Unintentionally, I fell into <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32294951.The_Gravity_of_Us__Elements___4_" title="The Gravity of Us (Elements, #4) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gravity of Us</a> (a brilliant book, btw) and with the warm fuzzies still swirling in my heart, I sought out other books by BC. <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29963453.The_Silent_Waters__Elements___3_" title="The Silent Waters (Elements, #3) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">The Silent Waters</a> came up with glowing reviews, so, I hopped onto the train. Part one was too funny for words with both protagonists, Maggie and Brooks, meeting and engaging with each other as very young kids. Too cute.</b><br /><br />The book takes a dark turn when Maggie witnesses and endures a terrible tragedy. A tragedy which impacted, for 18 long years, her life and family. <br /><br /><b>Unlike other reviewers who disliked this plot arc, I had no problem with the believability of Maggie's PTSD. A child's mind simply cannot process trauma in the manner that an adult would have done. It broke my heart.</b><br /><br />That being said, the duration of her psychological disorder was entirely too long. Add to that the characterization of Maggie's parents, the other "adults", and all I felt was a disconnect with the story as a whole.<br /><br />It seemed entirely too unbelievable that any parent would allow a 10-year-old regress into such a deep state of dissonance, much less one that sustains for 18 years.<br /><br />Then the pace of the story simply ebbed, with little progress made for nearly 50% of the book. I was frustrated by and for Maggie. If she could upload a video to Youtube, why didn't she research her condition? How could she have read in excess of 800 books and not once been interested in seeking help FOR HERSELF?<br /><br /><b>Where there no psychologists that could have made house calls? Additionally, did Maggie ever receive requisite health care? I mean, she was 10 at the time of the incident. Did she never fall ill? Orthodontic care?</b> <br /><br />So many questions.<br /><br />The love story itself was, in fact, uninspired and dare I say, predictable. I simply could not connect with them; moreover, the dialogue was insipid and cliche.<br /><br />Let's not even speak of the resolution. 20 years? And that's how you resolve the issues?<br /><br /><b>I didn't buy it.</b></blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="8437000627914509467" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1746472346?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=beautiful-cover">beautiful-cover</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=br">br</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1746472346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17675160134588690702"><b>One Million Beautiful Stars****************</b><br/><br/><i>(ARC kindly provided by author)<br/> (BR with my lovelies, Patty and Mel)</i><br/><br/>Brittainy C. Cherry wrote a book that spoke to my heart; every word consumed me, pained me, and enlighten me. The beauty and power of this novel felt unprecedented to me. An encouraging story that will forever stay engraved in my heart. <br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/638A27B7-847F-4E4B-BE67-0F3EBB8C8E73_zpskn4zlmwr.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474335508i/20583354._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 638A27B7-847F-4E4B-BE67-0F3EBB8C8E73_zpskn4zlmwr.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Maggie May was a girl that was always happy. She fell in love with a boy who gave her light, when she was scared of the darkness. When she was ten y</span>
  <span id="freeText17675160134588690702" style="display:none"><b>One Million Beautiful Stars****************</b><br><br><i>(ARC kindly provided by author)<br> (BR with my lovelies, Patty and Mel)</i><br><br>Brittainy C. Cherry wrote a book that spoke to my heart; every word consumed me, pained me, and enlighten me. The beauty and power of this novel felt unprecedented to me. An encouraging story that will forever stay engraved in my heart. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/638A27B7-847F-4E4B-BE67-0F3EBB8C8E73_zpskn4zlmwr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474335508i/20583354._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 638A27B7-847F-4E4B-BE67-0F3EBB8C8E73_zpskn4zlmwr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maggie May was a girl that was always happy. She fell in love with a boy who gave her light, when she was scared of the darkness. When she was ten years old she witness something horrific that took away her voice, her childhood and her faith in the world.<br><br>Brooks has only ever loved one girl; Maggie May. When they were little he used to get annoyed by her plans of their future wedding, but as they grew up, her smile was the one thing he couldn't live without.<br><br>Brooks and Maggie had a special bond, they could communicate through a simple look, or with a song. Their mutual love of music was something that solidified their bond through the years. Sharing lyrics and stories, and getting lost together in a world where there was no pain or darkness was the most precious thing they had in the world. <br><br>Life isn't easy for Maggie, fear always reign over her life. Guilt and pain affected every person around her. Her once easy relationship with her mom and sister is now almost non-existing , thanks to all the demons that live inside their little yellow house. <br><br>Luckily for Maggie Brooks is always there, also her dad, they are both her constant, the ones that no matter time or distance, no matter how many times she disappoints them by allowing fear to keep her trapped, they are always there, loving her. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/65FEDEE6-EEBF-493D-88EF-20F71BDD7708_zpsjf64dkio.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474335508i/20583355._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 65FEDEE6-EEBF-493D-88EF-20F71BDD7708_zpsjf64dkio.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The center of this book is love; beautiful, patient, loyal love. Through love Maggie will be able to break the shackles that have held her hostage, through love she will be able to give back to her family everything they gave to her, and because of love she will be able to forgive and mend those relationships that have suffered because of the silence. <br><br>This book was a hard read, but I can also tell you, that I swear I could see the pages of this book glow with a powerful shine, that will blind your eyes and fill your heart with hope and courage. <br><br>This book is a gift for those who lost their voice, to those who are afraid to speak and are missing out on life because they are scared. <br><br>A beautiful, romantic, and heartwarming novel full of music, that you are going to want to give to everyone in your life, and you will treasure forever. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453830803i/17878407.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <span id="freeText762167068747157840" style="display:none"><u>4.5 The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist ★'s</u> <br /><br /><i>“I needed her to know we’d make it work, no matter what. I needed her to know she was and always would be my biggest dream.”</i><br /><br />Ohhh my poor bleeding heart!!! That was one hell of an emotional ride! Again Brittainy C. Cherry managed to bring tears to my eyes within the first few chapters. Ugh. How in the world does she do that? Honestly, she knows just how to shatter my heart, then make it whole, then shatter my heart, and then make it whole all over again. The books that pull at the heartstrings will always be the best. The Silent Waters is just what you'd expect it to be when reading a Brittainy C. Cherry book. It was raw, emotional, and uplifting. Alrighty then, I'm onto the last book in this series The Gravity of Us :) :) <br /><br />♥By the way, that beautiful man on the cover is Luke Ditella!♥ (sigh)<br />I just love these covers!!<br /><br /><b>*Each book is a complete standalone with different characters.*</b></span>
