<div id="review_1762660154" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1762660154" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1762660154?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1762660154" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5247337750592322545">O.M.G. This book. <i>The Silent Waters</i> has owned my heart since the moment I read the first word. Cherry’s writing is so poetic and uniquely beautiful, I find myself getting lost in her stories. <br/><br/><i>The Silent Waters</i> is the story of Brooks and Maggie and believe me when I tell you their story is one of epic love, my favorite thing. Maggie and Brooks meet when they are five. Maggie’s father marries Katie and Brooks is her son’s best friend. They actually meet on the day Maggie arrives there with her dad</span>
  <span id="freeText5247337750592322545" style="display:none">O.M.G. This book. <i>The Silent Waters</i> has owned my heart since the moment I read the first word. Cherry’s writing is so poetic and uniquely beautiful, I find myself getting lost in her stories. <br><br><i>The Silent Waters</i> is the story of Brooks and Maggie and believe me when I tell you their story is one of epic love, my favorite thing. Maggie and Brooks meet when they are five. Maggie’s father marries Katie and Brooks is her son’s best friend. They actually meet on the day Maggie arrives there with her dad. The boys are playing video games and can barely spare her minute of their time, but as they get older Brooks feelings toward Maggie change. <br><br>This story follows Maggie and Brooks throughout years of their lives. It shows how over time they come to rely on each other and eventually fall in love. I don’t think there are words to do this story justice, because if you have read this book you know this story is about so much more than two kids growing up and falling in love. It’s about loss, it’s about love, it’s about hope, it’s about friendship, it’s about perseverance and sacrifice. This is an honest story of how life isn’t always fair, but true love always wins. <br><br>When I first read <i>The Silent Waters</i> my heart felt like it had been ripped open. My heart was broken for how unjust life is and how I wanted to rescue these two fictional characters. That’s how you know a book is epic. You finish the story, go to bed, only to wake up thinking about two fictional characters that you cannot be convinced are not real. They stay with you long after you finish the last page because their story came to life for you. <br><br>In my opinion, there are two parts of what make a story unforgettable, an unforgettable plot and a beautifully written story, Cherry delivered on both accounts. First, I fell in love with Brooks and Maggie's story, because like I said it’s epic. Then came the unforgettable plot that left me broken and healed at the same time. That’s what Brittainy’s writing does, she tells an emotional heartfelt story that leaves you broken and whole at the same time. Her writing makes you stop and think and reread, not for clarification, but you so you can allow the words to really marinate, so you can feel every emotion. <br><br>I cannot recommend this book enough. It’s real and heartfelt. It’s about strength and finding your voice. This book made me feel on so many levels and made me fell that high that only awesome books can deliver. I should absolutely warn you, though, this book will cause a HUGE book hangover, but no worries it will be worth it. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>

<div id="review_1747769647" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1747769647" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1747769647?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=famous-wealthy-popular">famous-wealthy-popular</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=safe-with-exception">safe-with-exception</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=3-5-star">3-5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=disordered-mc">disordered-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=musician">musician</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=neighbors-live-with">neighbors-live-with</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1747769647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16726996867103444799"><b> 3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This is a tough one to rate for me. I did think it was one of those stories that you truly feel like these characters were soulmates-- which is what I really look for! I liked both characters, and I felt for their struggles and traumas. And I cried! That also tells me I connected at least on some level to the story! So that's all good...<br/><br/>I just had some issues with the reality of it at times. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I felt like the h's conditions were resolved with a snap of a </span></span>
  <span id="freeText16726996867103444799" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This is a tough one to rate for me. I did think it was one of those stories that you truly feel like these characters were soulmates-- which is what I really look for! I liked both characters, and I felt for their struggles and traumas. And I cried! That also tells me I connected at least on some level to the story! So that's all good...<br /><br />I just had some issues with the reality of it at times. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I felt like the h's conditions were resolved with a snap of a finger! She was experiencing some major PTSD like behavior to the point that she hadn't left her house in over 20 years, but after the H has an accident it was just ok. Now, I understand that sometimes a troubling event can cause agoraphobic people out of their comfort zone -- but for her to just be ok after that to go anywhere?!? Even to the extent of shopping around a new town and traveling with the H later?!? I didn't find that all that believable. Also, when she speaks it's like a switch has been flipped! Not talking for after 20+ years has to do some type of damage to the vocal cords, right?!? I'm nowhere near a doctor, and I am probably just talking out of my ass -- but to go from not talking at all into paragraph-long monologues just felt really unrealistic. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br /><br />So -- I'm really struggling with my rating on this one because on one hand I loved it, and on the other I didn't...I'm going to go with a 3.5 stars. I just don't think I can rate it any higher because of my issues with the believability.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Maggie and Brooks' story. Maggie and her Dad move in with her new step-mom (and her son a and daughter) when Maggie is 6. Brooks is her new step-brother's best friend. She is convinced that they will be married and has it all planned. After witnessing a traumatic event, Maggie is no longer the bubbly kid she was before and becomes a mute and agoraphobic. Brooks decides that he will always help her and tells her that he will always be her anchor. As they grow, so does their relationship. There are some events that separate them, but their love for each other never goes away. When they are reunited, they both serve as each other's saviors in getting through their struggles...and get a HEA.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Maggie and Brooks' POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. They've known each other since they were young children.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Brooks. I really liked him. I felt like he did need to allow her to explain herself before their separation more, and I was also disappointed with the OW -- but it WAS 10 years, so I guess I can give him a break ;)<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Maggie. LOVED her as a young child at the beginning. I felt like she was pretty strong overall considering her trauma, and I appreciated her loyalty and love for Brooks.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate. I was expecting more tears tbh. I did cry some, but it didn't turn into an ugly cry, and I never needed tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h pushes the H away when his band hits it big, and causes their long separation. The H also pushes the h away after his trauma. They both pursue the relationship at times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Low. More about emotional connection rather than the physical act.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Not really. I wouldn't say it was fade to black, but it had minimal descriptions.<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Not sure there was any mention of safe sex practices.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes, but mild <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H is with OW for a while (not sure it said specifically how long) during the separation with the h. She shows up once after they broke-up and has a conversation with the h, but it was pretty mild drama.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for ~10 years. The H has at least one other long-term partner that we know of, and the h doesn't have any.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Murder, h is mute after trauma (PTSD type behavior), anxiety/panic attacks, agoraphobia, and alcoholism. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had good closure with a jump ahead epilogue and a HEA ending. I do wish that we saw them as an actual couple after both of them healed more, seen how they navigated their new realities, or even experienced some of her "to do" list...but that's me being greedy again ;)<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> It was part of my kindle unlimited subscription.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd call this <u>Safe with exception</u><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the H and the h pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a ~10 year separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1617257085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12856945516142227140"><br/><b>*****5 Stars*****</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“The world keeps spinning because your heartbeat exists.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475410455i/20718298._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>What a beautiful and moving story. I honestly can’t remember the last story I read which moved me in such a powerful way. “The Silent Waters” was inspiring, touching, heartbreaking and filled with a deep and profound love. “The Silent Waters” is the third instalment to the “Elements” series, but can be read as a standalone. I have loved all of Brittainy C. Cherry’s books that I have read. They always have the ability </span>
  <span id="freeText12856945516142227140" style="display:none"><br><b>*****5 Stars*****</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“The world keeps spinning because your heartbeat exists.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475410455i/20718298._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What a beautiful and moving story. I honestly can’t remember the last story I read which moved me in such a powerful way. “The Silent Waters” was inspiring, touching, heartbreaking and filled with a deep and profound love. “The Silent Waters” is the third instalment to the “Elements” series, but can be read as a standalone. I have loved all of Brittainy C. Cherry’s books that I have read. They always have the ability to make me feel so many different emotions. This story completely blew me away and I know this is one story that will stay with me forever. <br><br>Maggie May Riley was such an outgoing child who was full of energy. She always looked on the bright side and let nothing get her down. Her father Eric, had a love for his daughter which was so special; they had such a strong bond. Eric falls in love with a woman and moves the two of them to live with his new love and her two children. This is where she first met her new brother’s best friend, Brooks and he really captured her attention. <br><br><b>
  <i>“This time is forever.”</i>
</b><br><br>When Maggie May was ten years old, her voice was stolen from her through traumatic circumstances. Imagine being so consumed with fear, that you lose your ability to speak and constantly feel as if you are being choked. Maggie is a character I instantly fell in love with from the beginning when we were first introduced to her at the age of six. I loved reading about her story and the moments she experienced which forever changed her life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475411542i/20718438._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>“She’d be the one girl I’d love until forever. No matter how life tried to change us.”</i>
</b><br><br>Brooks is one of the most amazing characters I have ever had the privilege to read. He is sweet, patient, kind and understanding. He shares his love of music with Maggie and vows to show her the world. He’s her best friend and her anchor and he loves her deeply. Maggie and Brooks have the kind of love most people only dream of; they are the reason romance novels were invented. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Someday you’re going to see the whole wide world, Maggie May, and on that day, when you step outside breathe in your first breath, I want you to find me. No matter what, find me because I’m going to be the one to show it to you. I’m going to help you cross things off your to-do list. I’m going to show you the whole wide world.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475410984i/20718394._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>“The Silent Waters” was such a phenomenal read. Brittainy knows how to draw out absolutely every emotion from me. Her writing is outstanding and quite poetic. Her beautiful words will stay with me forever. There was nothing I didn’t like about this story. It was pure perfection. I urge anyone who has not read this one as yet, to do so especially if you love emotional, heartbreaking, inspirational stories with lovable characters and a deeply profound story. I also urge anyone who reads the book to please take the time to read Brittainy C. Cherry’s authors note at the end of the book, which is truly inspiring. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ve had many moments in my lifetime, moments that changed me, challenged me, moments that scared me and engulfed me. However, the biggest ones – the most heartbreaking and breathtaking ones – all included her.”</i>
</b><br></span>

Cherry <br><b>GENRE:</b> CONTEMPORARY ROMANCE<br><b>CHAPTERS:</b> Prologue | 45 | Epilogue <br><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> 23rd, September 2016<br><br><b>MY RATING: 4 STARS</b><br><br><b> BUDDY READ WITH </b> -❥Chatterbooks book blog ❥ <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2112iyv" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>THE SILENT WATERS:</b> Even though it states that this is part of a series it can be read as a complete standalone. Spoken in Dual Perspectives Brooks &amp; Maggie May <br><br>In the <b>'Prologue'</b> we meet young Maggie, in the year <b>2004</b> at six years old, her little family which consists of herself and her father are moving in with Katie her father's new fiancee, the first night she wakes up her new brother's best friend who was sleeping over, Brooks who lives right across the road, he comes into her room to see if she's ok and once he hears that she's scared of the dark, he goes and gets a night light for her, which is shaped like a rocket ship.<br><br><b> Moments.<br><br>Our lives are a collection of moments. Some utterly painful and full of yesterday's hurts. Some beautifully hopeful and full of tomorrow's promises. </b><br><br> <a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2090ugp" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474180921i/20564364.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i>
  <b> I felt protected by a rocket ship given to me by a boy I've just met. </b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=27zahjo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474492472i/20607459._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It all started with a rocket ship night light and a boy who didn't know her who came to her rescue. A little girls imagination ran wild, in 2008 ten year old Maggie declared her love for Brooks and claimed him as hers, even going as far as organising the wedding of the century. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2090ugp" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474180921i/20564364.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i>
  <b> What to you think about the colours purple and pink for the ceremony? <br>We should probably move in together, but I'm too young to have a mortgage.<br>Maybe we can stay with your parents until you get a steady job to support me and our pets. </b>
</i><br><br>I think the author has captured the true essence of a young girls first crush perfectly. Poor Brooks didn't know what hit him, he had nowhere to run, like a deer caught in the headlights he just went along with her hair brained ideas even though he declared he didn't like her one bit. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=i6crx1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474492472i/20607460._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> We are not getting married<br>We are not having pets.<br>We aren't even friends.<br>I HATE YOU MAGGIE MAY </i><br><br>The day where the ceremony was to take place was the day she lost her voice, lost her will to speak, lost the true essence of her innocence. From that day onwards she became to scared to leave the house and was home schooled from that day onwards by her step mother. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2090ugp" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474180921i/20564364.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i>
  <b> I was about to marry a boy who didn't know it yet, <br>but was going to be my best friend once we made it to our ten year anniversary.<br>He probably needed those ten years to realize he did indeed want to be my husband.<br>and we'd obviously live happily ever after. </b>
</i><br><br>This progresses through the ages until Maggie is Twenty-Eight, from the age of ten to now nothing really changed in her life, until one traumatic event made her take the steps to break the chains binding her to the house where she'd imprisoned herself to for a lifetime. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2090ugp" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474180921i/20564364.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i>
  <b> If you decide to never speak again.<br>You'll always have someone around to hear you Maggie.<br>I'll always be there to listen to your silence. </b>
</i><br><br>I crazy loved the early stages of Brooks and Maggie's friendship, her crazy railroading antics to claim this man to her were hilarious. I fell for these two characters hard. What was so refreshing with this book was for the fact that Brooks wasn't a broken down hero where she strived to fix him which made this even more unique. <br><br>There is no better feeling in the world than to pick up a book to find yourself transported to a world of feels. And this book delivers that tenfold. I've only been a relatively new follower of this authors due to this series. Her penmanship is outstanding, she brings all her characters to life with how the storyline flows effortlessly. Each book is beyond unique, if you haven't read this authors works before I urge you to take that leap, you won't be disappointed, she may even become one of your most favourite authors to follow like she fast became mine.<br><br>If I were to claim a <b>#BOOKBOYFRIEND</b> it would be Brooks, damn that guy just had the patience of a saint, a heart of gold, he pretty much had everything going for him, he stole my heart and hasn't given it back. Loved his character. <br><br>* TEASERS USED ARE OFF THE AUTHORS FB PAGE *<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34j24ye" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474325645i/20582486._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1769231634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9855174771579684584"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 from Elements series<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475133053i/20684642._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maggie May Riley was a precocious young girl. Her happy and bubbly personality captured the hearts of people around her. But a traumatic experience took away her voice and locked her up in her personal prison and forever changed the course of her life and her loved ones.<br/><br/>Brooks Tyler Griffin was the boy that captured Maggie's innocent young heart. He went from incredibly annoyed to utterly smit</span>
  <span id="freeText9855174771579684584" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 from Elements series<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475133053i/20684642._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maggie May Riley was a precocious young girl. Her happy and bubbly personality captured the hearts of people around her. But a traumatic experience took away her voice and locked her up in her personal prison and forever changed the course of her life and her loved ones.<br><br>Brooks Tyler Griffin was the boy that captured Maggie's innocent young heart. He went from incredibly annoyed to utterly smitten by her tenacity. When she was sinking, he was there to keep her from drowning. But sometimes a rogue wave could crash by and pull you even deeper under.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once in a while I came across books that punched me in the heart and left a lasting beautiful ache. This book is one of them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>I loved how he could see me when the rest of the world forgot I existed.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Maggie was such an adorable kid. So young and innocent, and to see that bright light dimmed away really hurt. I could relate to her on every level and I understand her coping mechanism.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Why couldn’t I fix her ? Why couldn’t I take her pain and make it my own?</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Brooks was someone anyone could use as a friend. He was kind, loyal and patient. I love how much selfless he was, even if it hurt him to do so.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475133343i/20684703.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two latched to my heart since the very beginning. Their letters both as kids and adults did things to my heart haha! I understand the actions of every single characters in this book no matter heroes or villains. And, oh I adore Mrs. Boone!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Being in love with someone didn’t mean you only loved them during the sunbeams. It meant you stood by their side during the cloudy nights, too.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I really like the story and how it turned around, but I wasn't fond of the last 10% or so. It was too much too soon. I would prefer if it was wrapped up with a little more layers to make it more realistic.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>That night I realized a few things about life. Sometimes the rain was more pleasing than the sun. Sometimes the hurt was more fulfilling than the healing. And sometimes the pieces of a puzzle were more beautiful when scattered apart.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Silent Waters is a beautiful story of hurt and healing which reminds us no matter how strong we are, we could always use an anchor to secure us from drifting away.<br><br><b>Note:</b><br><i>I very rarely use music in my review but this song wouldn't leave my head while I read this. So I decided to include it. The lyrics is perfect for the story.</i><br><br>I Will Be by Leona Lewis<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=L8q6f4CvINE">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=L8q6f...</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>I will be, all that you want<br>And get myself together<br>Cause you keep me from falling apart<br>All my life, I'll be with you forever<br>To get you through the day<br>And make everything OK</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Standalone books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564446.The_Air_He_Breathes__Elements___1_" title="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1441375261s/25564446.jpg" alt="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26615962.The_Fire_Between_High___Lo__Elements___2_" title="The Fire Between High &amp; Lo (Elements, #2) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1456332708s/26615962.jpg" alt="The Fire Between High &amp; Lo (Elements, #2) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29963453.The_Silent_Waters__Elements___3_" title="The Silent Waters (Elements, #3) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1472832783s/29963453.jpg" alt="The Silent Waters (Elements, #3) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><b>✨ ♔ ✨ . . . (F)BR With Loyda . . . ✨ ♔ ✨</b><br><br><i>Copy won from Amazon giveaway</i><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454304059i/17942101.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1642779480" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1642779480" />
    <a title="Wil Loves Books!" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3232198-wil-loves-books"><img alt="Wil Loves Books!" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467223384p2/3232198.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1642779480?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wil Loves Books!" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wil Loves Books!" href="/user/show/3232198-wil-loves-books">Wil Loves Books!</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=on-paperback">on-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=priority-tbr">priority-tbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=on-kindle">on-kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1642779480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9724010075392789987"><br/><br/><strong>
  <em> “Not all broken things need to be fixed. Sometimes they just need to be loved. It would be a shame if only people who were whole were deserving of love.”</em>
</strong><br/><br/>This book was simply amazing. Every time I read a Brittainy Cherry book, I fall more and more in love with her writing. She doesn’t just tell you a story, she takes you on an amazing journey. These characters, they’re so raw and real, and so amazingly developed, you can’t help but fall in love with them. Brittainy is a one-click author for </span>
  <span id="freeText9724010075392789987" style="display:none"><br><br><strong>
  <em> “Not all broken things need to be fixed. Sometimes they just need to be loved. It would be a shame if only people who were whole were deserving of love.”</em>
</strong><br><br>This book was simply amazing. Every time I read a Brittainy Cherry book, I fall more and more in love with her writing. She doesn’t just tell you a story, she takes you on an amazing journey. These characters, they’re so raw and real, and so amazingly developed, you can’t help but fall in love with them. Brittainy is a one-click author for me, if she writes it, I’ll read it.<br><br><strong>
  <em>“The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist.” </em>
</strong><br><br>The Silent Waters is Book 3 on The Element Series, although this is a series of books that revolve around the elements, Book 1 (The Air He Breathes), Book 2 (The Fire Between High and Lo), these books are complete standalones. The books are totally unrelated and the characters do not cross books. So you could skip the previous 2 books, although I strongly suggest you read them all. You will not be disappointed, they’re all amazing.<br><br>The Silent Waters tells the story of Maggie May and Brooks, neighbors, childhood best friends, and eventually lovers as they go through the best and worst experiences of their lives. From the prologue through the epilogue the story spans a few decades. Now, I’m not sure how much I want to say, I know I must sound like a broken record but sometimes you need to go into some books blind and discover them by yourself. And I definitely thing this is one of those. So, I will try not to spoil major plot points.<br><br><strong>
  <em>“I hadn’t known you could hear someone’s voice so clearly in the silent moments.”</em>
</strong><br><br>Maggie May is a beautiful, smart and lively child that experiences a traumatic event that marks it forever. She is such a beautiful and amazingly developed character, I dare you not to fall in love with her. I felt so much for her and her struggles. She was truly remarkable.<br><br><strong>
  <em>“I didn’t always feel like smiling, but Brooks? He made me feel as if smiling was all I ever wanted to do.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>“He drove me crazy. His hold, his touch, his voice, his words. Everything about his soul lit me on fire, and I was proud to burn beside him.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>“I loved him. I wasn’t certain when it had happened. I wasn’t certain if it was a group of moments collected over time or simply the heroic act he’d performed while I was sleeping, but it didn’t matter. It didn’t matter when, or why, or how it had happened. It didn’t matter how many moments gathered together to form the love. It didn’t matter if it was right or wrong.”</em>
</strong><br><br>And Brooks, what can I say about Brooks. He’s amazing and beautiful, patient and understanding. He was Maggie’s anchor, her beacon of light through the darkness. He was hers, completely. I loved everything about Brooks. He also went through a dark time and was able to overcome everything life threw at him. He’s definitely at the top of by Brittainy heroes, along with Logan.<br><br><strong>
  <em> “She quietly chuckled and rolled her eyes. I loved that. I loved when she laughed, even though it was so quiet. It was the closest thing I had to her voice.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>“It was freeing to feel so much with someone who felt it too. It was during those moments that I felt I learned the most about her. It was in those moments that she learned the most about me.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>“I love you, Maggie May,” he whispered, looking into my eyes. “I mean, I keep staring at you, and I can’t help but think, ‘Wow. I’m really loving this girl right now.’ You know? Everything about you, I love. The easy days and the hard ones, too. Maybe I love you even more on the hard days. I’m not sure if I’m supposed to say it yet, because I don’t know if you’re ready, but that’s okay. You take all the time you need, but I wanted to let you know, because when you love someone, I think you gotta scream it, otherwise the love in your chest becomes a bit heavy. It weighs you down, and you start wondering if the other person loves you, too. I’m not worried about that, though. I’m just sitting here, next to you, looking at the small freckles on your face that most people miss, thinkin’ about how much I love you in this moment.”</em>
</strong><br><br><br>The love between them was definitely my favorite part of the book, it was so pure, so real, so powerful. It’s what kept them both going in difficult times and what kept me hopeful that they totally deserved a happy ending.<br><br><strong>
  <em>“Do you promise me the same type of love I’ve read about in my books? He shook his head, yawning. His arms wrapped around me, pulling me closer as I became engulfed by his warmth. “No, Maggie May. I promise you so much more.””</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“Maggie May, you’re my favorite song.” </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>Being in love with someone didn’t mean you only loved them during the sunbeams. It meant you stood by their side during the cloudy nights, too.</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“I was thankful for it all, the quiet moments and the painful ones, too. I was thankful for her willingness to allow me to bleed out against her. I was thankful for her bleeding out onto my soul.”</em>
</strong><br><br>I also loved all of the secondary characters, they were all a great addition to the story and made it more complete. I loved Maggie's dad, her brother and sister, the band mates and especially Mrs. Boone. <br><br>This book, it will hook you from the prologue all the way to the author’s note at the end. I felt a lot while reading this book. Happiness, sadness, fear, frustration, love, anger. It was truly a journey. It was also so moving and inspirational. And beautiful, just beautiful. As you can see, I have so many highlights, it’s not even funny. So much beauty in those words!<br><br><strong>
  <em>“That’s what true love meant to me. True love meant you could laugh at mistakes. True love meant you could whisper secrets. True love meant you never had to dance alone.”</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>“Love didn’t come with guidelines. It flowed into a person with only hope as its current. There wasn’t a list of rules to follow, making sure you cared for it correctly. It didn’t give you instructions to keep it pure. It simply showed up quietly, praying you wouldn’t let it slip away.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br>So, needless to say, I absolutely, 100% recommend The Silent Waters. It’s one of my favorite books this year. It has all the feels and you will not be disappointed! And if you haven’t read the other 2 books in this series, do me a favor and pick those up too, they’re amazing.  I can’t wait for the next book in this series.<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“What he didn’t know was that he was the biggest adventure of my life. He was my favorite journey, my anchor that always led me home.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“Moments. Humans always remember the moments. We recall the steps that led us to where we were meant to be. The words that inspired or crushed us. The incidents that scarred us and swallowed us whole. I’ve had many moments in my lifetime, moments that changed me, challenged me, moments that scared me and engulfed me. However, the biggest ones—the most heartbreaking and breathtaking ones—all included her.”</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444752880i/16547832.png" alt="Wil" width="200" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br><br><strong>*An ARC was generously provided by the author in exchange for an honest review*</strong><br><br> <br><p>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474877124i/20650228._SX540_.jpg" alt="the-silent-waters-teaser-2" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><strong>JOIN THE SISTERHOOD! FIND US ON: </strong><strong><a href="https://www.facebook.com/tbbsisterhood" rel="nofollow noopener">FACEBOOK</a> / <a href="https://www.instagram.com/tbbsisterhood" rel="nofollow noopener">INSTAGRAM</a> / <a href="https://twitter.com/tbbsisterhood" rel="nofollow noopener">TWITTER</a> / <a href="http://tbbsisterhood.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">BLOG</a></strong></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1762294033" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1762294033" />
    <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog"><img alt="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420222674p2/38657470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1762294033?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32070295-the-silent-waters">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=we-will-rock-you">we-will-rock-you</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1762294033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18435708862861237910">Fair warning. This review is probably going to suck because there’s nothing I can say that will adequately convey the way <i>The Silent Waters</i> affected me. I admit I was hesitant to read it. I wasn’t sure I was emotionally prepared for a book whose synopsis clearly states that it’s heartbreaking and tragic. However, I have absolutely no regrets about reading this book other than the fact that I’m now left with a massive book hangover.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist.</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText18435708862861237910" style="display:none">Fair warning. This review is probably going to suck because there’s nothing I can say that will adequately convey the way <i>The Silent Waters</i> affected me. I admit I was hesitant to read it. I wasn’t sure I was emotionally prepared for a book whose synopsis clearly states that it’s heartbreaking and tragic. However, I have absolutely no regrets about reading this book other than the fact that I’m now left with a massive book hangover.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Every single character is so well developed I’d swear they are real people. I felt as if they were <b>my</b> father, <b>my</b> best friend, <b>my</b> sister, and <b>my</b> neighbor. The relationships between all characters—even the seemingly minor ones—are explored to their fullest advantage, making them integral to the entire storyline. I guarantee that you will ship Maggie and Brooks hard. Really hard.<br><br>I’m going to be completely honest. This story wrecked me at times. You may want to have some tissues nearby since there is sorrow, but there are also plenty of moments of laughter, hope, encouragement and, above all, love. I’m telling you this book has all the feels!<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He deserved to be loved out loud, and my love was a whisper in the wind that obviously only he could hear.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Brittainy C. Cherry’s writing is superb, and the plot development is so well constructed that its impact sneaks up on you bit by bit. This is definitely my favorite work of hers I’ve read so far.<br><br>My advice to would-be readers is to risk your heart. You will be rewarded with a wonderfully inspirational journey. I can say with utmost certainty that <i>The Silent Waters</i> is one of the most devastatingly poignant books I’ve read this year. I will hold the characters and this story in my heart for a long time.<br><br><b>Recommended for fans of:</b><br>Tear jerkers<br>Best friends<br>Survivors<br>Rock stars<br><br><i>**ARC received in exchange for an honest review.**</i><br><br><a href="http://readingfrenzyblog.com" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458784026i/18530130.jpg" alt="Reading Frenzy Book Blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18435708862861237910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1752847611" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1752847611" />
    <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison"><img alt="Jeannine Allison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488001283p2/30604562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1752847611?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeannine Allison" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison">Jeannine Allison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=swoon">swoon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=signed-paperbacks">signed-paperbacks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=tatted-heroes">tatted-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=sweet-guys">sweet-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=love-the-heroine">love-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=bawling-like-a-baby">bawling-like-a-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=99c-or-free">99c-or-free</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1752847611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1283989091069352415">First things first, I'm OBSESSED with these quotes <3 Normally I save this for later, but these are some of my favorite words ever!! :)<i>
  <blockquote>"The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist."</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>What if I wasn't broken? What if this was just me?</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>"Not all broken things need to be fixed. Sometimes they just need to be loved. It would be a shame if only people who were whole were deserving of love."</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>Her heartbeats were made for me, and mine for hers.</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>Sometimes I wondered if there was a</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText1283989091069352415" style="display:none">First things first, I'm OBSESSED with these quotes &lt;3 Normally I save this for later, but these are some of my favorite words ever!! :)<i>
  <blockquote>"The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist."</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>What if I wasn't broken? What if this was just me?</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>"Not all broken things need to be fixed. Sometimes they just need to be loved. It would be a shame if only people who were whole were deserving of love."</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>Her heartbeats were made for me, and mine for hers.</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>Sometimes I wondered if there was anything to truly figure out, or if we were all walking around looking for a reason when no reason truly existed.</blockquote>
</i>I mean, SERIOUSLY, this author is the reason I love words &lt;3 <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492299383ra/22503577.gif" width="500" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, so this will be very similar to my review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564446.The_Air_He_Breathes__Elements___1_" title="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">The Air He Breathes</a>. I finished this in a day, becoming hooked from the very beginning. The first part of this book was adorable. I loved seeing the younger versions of them. Maggie broke my heart... <i>
  <blockquote>"You know, I've always wanted another daughter," she said, brushing my hair. I didn't say it, but I had always wanted a mama, too.</blockquote>
</i>But she was also really funny!<i>
  <blockquote>I think that's <s>stupid</s> stupid, but I also know that my mama says all men are stupid, so it's not your fault. It's in your DNA.</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>Cheryl and squirrels had a few things in common. For example, squirrels liked nuts, and Cheryl was completely nuts if she thought for a second Brooks would like her before me.</blockquote>
</i>I was smiling so big in the first 10% on this book. And I loved how she connected everything about Brooks and Maggie together.<i>
  <blockquote>I hated Maggie May. I wished there were a bigger word to describe my feelings for the annoying, loud-mouthed girl who had been following me around lately, but hate seemed to be the only thing that came to mind whenever she stood near me.</blockquote>
</i><i>
  <blockquote>I loved Brooks Tyler. I wished there were a bigger word to describe my feelings for the handsome, rude boy who had been kissing me lately, but love seemed to be the only thing that came to mind whenever he stood near me.</blockquote>
</i>I just thought this was the most precious thing, even though Brooks says he "hates" her. And we realize just how much he cares for Maggie when tragedy befalls her. Honestly I was swooning SO freaking hard, which felt a little creepy since he was ten-years-old... but he was just so sweet!!<blockquote>
  <i>I'd do anything to bring her beautiful ugly smiles back to the world.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>I missed the one thing that had annoyed me for so long. I missed her voice.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"I want you to smile again. I want you to have the things you always wanted, and I'm gonna work hard to make sure you get them, too, even if it's a dog named Skippy and a cat named Jam. I want you to know… I need you to know that even if you decide to never speak again, you'll always have someone around to hear you, Maggie. All right? I'll always be there to listen to your silence."</i>
</blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492327752ra/22505613.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall I liked the two of them. There were some actions (of Brooks) at the end that I didn't love, but they didn't really make sense to me so I kind of overlooked them in terms of what they meant for his character.<br><br><b>Other random things I loved:</b><br><br><u>Cheryl's development</u><br>She is one of my favorite side characters ever! She pissed me off at times for sure, but I'm always craving dimensional characters. Ones I'll love and be pissed off at in equal measures, and she delivered! I seriously loved her and wouldn't mind reading about her again.<blockquote>
  <i>"I want to fight for you, for people like you. I want to fight for those who don't have a voice, but are screaming to be heard."</i>
</blockquote><u>All the reading quotes</u><blockquote>
  <i>"But you're only mad because you know I'm right... You can't just read these books and think that means you're living. It's their story, not yours, and it's heartbreaking to watch someone so young toss away their chance at writing their own story."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Reading was both a gift and a curse for me. Those books made me able to escape into a world I'd never experienced, but at the same time, they reminded me of all the things I'd been missing.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Dozens and dozens of adventures I hoped to one day experience were ruined, and I couldn’t help but to burst into tears. I knew it seemed dramatic, but those books, those characters— they were my friends, my safe haven, my protection. That list was my promise of tomorrow. And now I had nothing.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"All this time I thought you were reading to escape the world, but now I know, you didn't read to escape it; you read to discover it."</i>
</blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492329157ra/22505725.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Things I didn't understand:</b><br><br><u>Brook's other relationships</u><br>This is minor, like REALLY minor, so I don't want to scare anyone. There's no cheating and most of the mentions are just in passing. But I guess that's why I didn't understand it. It didn't really add anything to the story. And whenever I read "I've loved you since childhood" stories, I'm always thrown when they're with other people. Like, at the end of part one, Brooks thinks...<blockquote>
  <i>In that moment, I knew she had been right about everything all along. She was right about me, and her, and us. She'd be the one girl I'd love until forever. No matter how life tried to change us.</i>
</blockquote>I know I'm probably being harsh/unrealistic. I know Maggie, being a mute and recluse, doesn't make for prime girlfriend material. And Brooks is a teenage boy. I know. I get it. But I just always have a problem with the characters knowing they're "meant to be" but still seeing others :/ If you're old enough to know that you want to be with this person forever, you're old enough to take responsibility for it. I'm not an avid safety ganger and I definitely didn't think less of Brooks, so this wasn't a big issue at all. But I'm always confused by it and just thought I'd mention it.<br><br><u>Maggie's "healing"</u><br>I will never pretend to understand how another person experiences a mental illness. Even with a mental illness myself, I know how varied these illnesses are. They're very tricky. That being said, I didn't buy how fast her recovery came.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She'd been going through this for TWENTY years, and suddenly she decides she can get over it all? For Brooks? Maggie convinces herself to leave for Brooks and uses his love as her guide.<i><blockquote>Remembering that our love was louder than my past moments.</blockquote></i>It's a nice thought. That love can overcome anything, but it's unrealistic and I don't like the message it sends. Maggie should have taken that step <i>for herself</i>.<br><br>*I would also imagine there would be some damage since she didn't use her vocal chords for twenty years, no? I really have no clue... but even if there wasn't damage, I can't imagine she'd talk so much/so freely so soon. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><u>The OTT drama at the end</u><br>I had the same problem in the other two, and probably will in the fourth as well. Everything is going great and then at 80% there's some crazy drama thrown in that seems completely unnecessary. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Everything from the separation to Brooks accident was hard for me to swallow. They're separated for ten years and yet they come together <i>very quickly</i>, almost as if no time has passed. I understand her wanting to let him go for his career, but I think ten years was far too long. Especially given how fast they reunited.<br><br>Then there's his accident. Brooks is injured in a boating accident and injures his hand (the one he uses for playing). His misplace guilty, minor binge with alcohol, and rude behavior toward Maggie really didn't work for me. I thought his accident was blown out of proportion. He wasn't doing drugs and trashed a hotel room or something. He was drinking and having a good time, and an <i>accident</i> happened. I didn't really believe that so many people would bash on him and I didn't understand why he was so hard on himself. And how he treated Maggie? I hated it, and it was so out of character :(<blockquote><i>He'd stumble home sloppy drunk so many times, and come my way, telling me how pathetic I was, and how I should’ve moved on with my life, because we’d never be together. We'd never have a future.</i></blockquote>
<blockquote><i>"Stop embarrassing yourself, Magnet. This isn't going to happen. Don't you have some kind of list to get to?" He snickered and fell backward against the wall. "Or are you too afraid to do anything on your own?"</i></blockquote>I just thought this all happened way too quickly to ever develop into something I could believe. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Even though I had some niggles, I really did enjoy this! The beginning was just perfection and the writing was breathtaking as always. I'm excited to start the fourth one soon &lt;3<br><br>Safety: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No OM and minimal OW drama. Brooks has a couple girlfriends when he knows her as a teen, and one (mentioned) long-term girlfriend during their ten-year separation. The latter girlfriend has a brief conversation with Maggie, but it wasn't heated or catty. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Closure: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[A cute epilogue ten years later where they are married with children &lt;3 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1283989091069352415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Linda Kage" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3531137-linda-kage"><img alt="Linda Kage" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513777429p2/3531137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1762316601?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Linda Kage" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Linda Kage" href="/user/show/3531137-linda-kage">Linda Kage</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531137-linda-kage?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531137-linda-kage?shelf=yes-hea">yes-hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531137-linda-kage?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531137-linda-kage?shelf=2016-favorite">2016-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1762316601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer616268268040526516">I finished! And survived. This is going to be one of my favorite books ever! So beautiful. And that author's note... Wow. No wonder why Maggie May felt so relatable to me. Kinds of makes me love Brittainy Cherry even more now. And really made me want to just contact my friends and hug them. <br/><br/>For some reason, I find this story comparable to Sweet Gum Tree, even though they don't really have much in common. I guess the way the characters started up young together and had to go through their tragedi</span>
  <span id="freeText616268268040526516" style="display:none">I finished! And survived. This is going to be one of my favorite books ever! So beautiful. And that author's note... Wow. No wonder why Maggie May felt so relatable to me. Kinds of makes me love Brittainy Cherry even more now. And really made me want to just contact my friends and hug them. <br /><br />For some reason, I find this story comparable to Sweet Gum Tree, even though they don't really have much in common. I guess the way the characters started up young together and had to go through their tragedies until they could make it together at the end is what made me compare them. Both were so good! My heart is happy yet sad, but fulfilled all at the same time after reading this! It's not just a story; it's an experience. I'm glad I read it. <br /><br /><br />Half-way Through Review : (Sep 24, 2016, 55% finished!)<br /><br />I swear, reading this book is like wading out into the ocean! At first, it was like a nice relaxing, frivolous day on the beach. The scenes of Brooks and Maggie when they're six and ten were so cute and fun and easy to read. Eager for more, I just kept sifting my toes through the sand, page after page and straying farther from the shore until I encountered the shocking drop off moment, when things got more intense and deeper. Wow. Did not see that coming. But it was all still good. My feet could still touch bottom, and the water--I mean, the story, sorry--felt so nice, so I just kept swimming and swimming, unable to put it down, once again flipping page after page until ack, this all feels so deep and kind of like I'm drowning in my own tears from how sad everything is, only to look up and realize I'm out in the middle of the freaking ocean now, no land in sight, and this book is bottomless. Feels like sink or swim time. If this story doesn't kill me, I'm going to be forced to climb out of the Silent Waters at the end a much stronger person. What an experience. PS-and yes, I've been up since 1:30am, reading (it's five now) so I might possibly be talking in crazy lingo. Still an awesome book, though! </span>
  <a data-text-id="616268268040526516" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1761191720" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1761191720" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1761191720?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=terribly-sad">terribly-sad</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1761191720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5130925168387181407"><b> <i>" Love didn't come with guidelines. It flowed into a person with only hope as its current. There wasn't a list of rules to follow, making sure you cared for it correctly. It didn't give you instructions to keep it pure. It simply showed up quietly, praying you wouldn't let it slip away" </i></b><br/><br/>This book was heartbreaking. I was overwhelmed from the very beginning, but my excitement to read The Silent Waters was stronger, so I pushed myself although I don't like sad books. <br/>This is the story of Maggie a</span>
  <span id="freeText5130925168387181407" style="display:none"><b> <i>" Love didn't come with guidelines. It flowed into a person with only hope as its current. There wasn't a list of rules to follow, making sure you cared for it correctly. It didn't give you instructions to keep it pure. It simply showed up quietly, praying you wouldn't let it slip away" </i></b><br><br>This book was heartbreaking. I was overwhelmed from the very beginning, but my excitement to read The Silent Waters was stronger, so I pushed myself although I don't like sad books. <br>This is the story of Maggie and Brooks, a young couple that knows each other since childhood, and from there on their feelings progressed. Well, from Maggie point of view for sure, but for Brooks it wasn't love at first sight! From the moment they met she had a huge crush on Brooks, but typical for any boy of his age, the resented her and tried to keep his distance. <br><br>I liked Maggie from the beginning, so chatty, smart and persistent. Her sweetness and innocence made me want to protect her and be her friend. Brooks on the other hand was rude to her, but his moments of weakness were adorable and you could feel that he was falling in love as well, although he was only 8. At that age a tragic event happens to Maggie , <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ leaving her without her voice  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. From there on, everything around changes, including the relationship with her family and Brooks. <br><br>The topic surrounding the book is fantastic and delivers such a strong message that leaves you lingering and wondering, because it so down to earth and unfortunately happens to so many children out there. PTSD is a very well known symptom after a traumatizing experience and parents need a lot of guidance in order to help their kids recover. Every one manifests in his own way and patience and love is needed in order to handle the aftermath. <br><br>From my point of view Maggie was left to be more time that it was recommended, until nothing could be done. The barriers lifted were too high and it took a lot of years for her to realize how to crack them. The panic and fear overcame her, leaving her without any choice than you stop all connection to the real world. <br><br>I loved her relationship with her father, it was really unique. They connected without words and I enjoyed the kind of bond that they had. Her relationship with her mother was kind of complicated for me because when guilt is involved, people tend to make a lot of mistakes and don't even realize it. She was so fierce in protecting Maggie that didn't understand that maybe she is not helping her, only lifting her barriers higher.<br> <br>As for Brooks, their connection was on an emotional level, a profound one, that makes you believe in true love and soul mates. After the incident with Maggie, they became best friends and were inseparable since. I enjoyed their development and the peak of their feeling for each other. Once realizing how in love they are, they managed to catch my attention, because their scenes were so intense and sweet. The amount of emotions put in their dialogues was amazing and I really ached for them, because they were so good together, in perfect harmony. They connected without words, only through music and eye contact. You could literary feel their love and I was hoping they get the happy ending they deserve. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475070301i/20677235._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I related myself to Maggie in the books aspect. Because of her isolation, her only gate to the world were her books. She has so in love with them, being absorbed into that universe, falling in love with the characters, crying and laughing with them. I feel the same way when I'm reading, it is impossible not to relate, feel and be part of the story. <br><br>The thing that I didn't enjoy was the tragic twist the writer included at the end of the book. I mean, there were so many sad events going on that another sad thing was not necessary from my point of view. But after thinking it better, it had to be included for the characters to have the needed closure, and the happy ending that they truly deserve. <br><br>A round of applause to Brittainy on her penmanship and the raw emotion she managed to pass on to the reader. I consider it being one of the most realistic and emotional books of 2016. <br><br>4 spinning stars for this one!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5130925168387181407" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1616807090?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15988565-fmabookreviews?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15988565-fmabookreviews?shelf=5-it-fed-my-addiction-stars">5-it-fed-my-addiction-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15988565-fmabookreviews?shelf=favorites-of-2016">favorites-of-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1616807090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer730565268890234896"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝I'll be your anchor. I'll help you stay grounded when you feel like you're drifting away.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>With the 3rd book in The Elements Series, Brittainy C. Cherry immerses her readers in so much thought provoking angsty-goodness, that tears are sure to flow, while hearts and minds are being opened.<br/><br/>Hands down a favorite of the year, I read this in one sitting. Ignoring all things that needed to be tended to, I dove head first into the characters and story that Cherry created, and didn't come up</span>
  <span id="freeText730565268890234896" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝I'll be your anchor. I'll help you stay grounded when you feel like you're drifting away.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />With the 3rd book in The Elements Series, Brittainy C. Cherry immerses her readers in so much thought provoking angsty-goodness, that tears are sure to flow, while hearts and minds are being opened.<br /><br />Hands down a favorite of the year, I read this in one sitting. Ignoring all things that needed to be tended to, I dove head first into the characters and story that Cherry created, and didn't come up for air until after her author note.<br /><blockquote><b><i>❝Do you promise me the same type of love I've read about in my books?❞</i></b> He shook his head, yawning. His arms wrapped around me, pulling me closer as I became engulfed by his warmth. <b><i>❝No, Maggie May. I promise you so much more.❞</i></b></blockquote><br />Once a gregarious and outgoing girl so full of life that she often annoyed those around her, Maggie Riley suddenly has her voice and security stripped from her. But always at her side, always willing to "listen to her silence", was Brooks Griffin. His patience, love, and friendship help her heal.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝I loved that about him. I loved how he could see me when the rest of the world forgot I existed.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />It was this love that pulled her from the shadows and made her fight for him when his own troubles occurred pulling him under. The fierceness of her devotion shocking him into facing his fears.<br /><br />This is a beautiful love story. It is about not taking situations or people at face value. It is about love so fierce, you will do anything to protect it and the one's you love.<br /><br />This author has an unforgettable talent. Her writing is breathtaking, her characters perfectly flawed and her stories are captivating. As with all her books, this story and these characters will stay with me long after I turn the last page.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝A person never reads an outstanding book twice and walks away with the same beliefs. An outstanding book always surprises you and awakens you to new ideas, new ways of looking at the world, no matter how many times the words have been read.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

          </div>
