        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1762426612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15837390238292030227"><b>RATING: 5+ thunderstorms and sunlight HEARTS!! <3</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1502828212i/23600847.jpg' width='400' height='310' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>The Silent Waters</i> is an absolutely breath-taking story, penned raw, heart-aching emotions threatening to drown us in their verisimilitude, but the underlying love story woven from the fragile threads of friendship into a stunning tapestry of true love keeping us afloat as its phantom fingers point to hope and a happy ending. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> True love meant you could laugh at mistakes.<br/>True love meant you could whisper secrets.<br/>True love meant you never had</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15837390238292030227" style="display:none"><b>RATING: 5+ thunderstorms and sunlight HEARTS!! &lt;3</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1502828212i/23600847.jpg" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>The Silent Waters</i> is an absolutely breath-taking story, penned raw, heart-aching emotions threatening to drown us in their verisimilitude, but the underlying love story woven from the fragile threads of friendship into a stunning tapestry of true love keeping us afloat as its phantom fingers point to hope and a happy ending. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> True love meant you could laugh at mistakes.<br>True love meant you could whisper secrets.<br>True love meant you never had to dance alone. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>What makes us fall madly in love with this tale is the animation of mental turmoil, emotional heartbreak, tender passion, and utter joy as a result of Ms. Cherry’s powerful prose, every word our captor, forcing us to experience the gamut of those emotions with the characters every step of the way. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “The world keeps spinning because your heartbeats exist.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Maggie and Brooks are both exquisite characters—individually, with complex dynamics that change and grow throughout the story as they both learn to navigate the best and worst experiences of their lives, yet their coupledom straightforward and natural making it evident right from the onset that they are meant for each other regardless of the multitude of reasons keeping them at a distance. The two of them together are enthralling from first to last page, their relationship—physical and emotional, romantic and platonic—dovetailing beautifully with their individual battles. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> That night I realized a few things about life. Sometimes the rain was more pleasing than the sun. Sometimes the hurt was more fulfilling than the healing. And sometimes the pieces of a puzzle were more beautiful when scattered apart. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, <i>The Silent Waters</i> is a sensational addition to this series, Maggie and Brooks’ story of friendship, hindered love and personal hardships is hard to read in the most gorgeous way, making this story and the two of them a couple hard to forget long after the end. <br><br><br><u>Other Fave Quotes:</u><br><br><b>
  <i>A person never reads an outstanding book twice and walks away with the same beliefs. An outstanding book always surprises you and awakens you to new ideas, new ways of looking at the world, no matter how many times the words have been read.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Those who believed in you when you didn’t believe in yourself were the ones to hold close. </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Maggie May, you’re my favorite song.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Being in love with someone didn’t mean you only loved them during the sunbeams. It meant you stood by their side during the cloudy nights, too. </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>What he didn’t know was that he was the biggest adventure of my life. He was my favourite journey, my anchor that always led me home. </i>
</b><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Posted: August 15, 2017</i>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1642752594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17159407892392711954"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474800073i/20642139._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='310' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am going to keep this short. Never in my life have I related to characters more than I have related to not only Brooks and Maggie, but her parents and her sister as well. <b>It’s incredible how I didn’t even realize that I needed a book like this in my life until I’ve closed its pages last night.</b> I rarely cry, I rarely connect with every single character in a book, I rarely feel my heart beating as loud as it gets just by reading words on a page, I rarely can’t sleep at night because I’m thinking</span>
  <span id="freeText17159407892392711954" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474800073i/20642139._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am going to keep this short. Never in my life have I related to characters more than I have related to not only Brooks and Maggie, but her parents and her sister as well. <b>It’s incredible how I didn’t even realize that I needed a book like this in my life until I’ve closed its pages last night.</b> I rarely cry, I rarely connect with every single character in a book, I rarely feel my heart beating as loud as it gets just by reading words on a page, I rarely can’t sleep at night because I’m thinking about a book I’ve finished that day… and yet, this book made me do all of the things listed above. I’ve finished it last night around 11.30pm and just sat and cried for fifteen minutes. I just needed to let all the emotions that this book made me feel out. I went to sleep, but I’ve lay awake for two hours thinking about every quote that I’ve highlighted, every scene that made my heart break a little.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474800073i/20642140._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In my opinion, this is the best book Brittainy has ever written. And I want to tell you something.<br><br><b>
  <i>Brittainy, your Maggie May says that words can change lives. She’s right.<br><br>I think you’ve just changed mine.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474800073i/20642141._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Thank you Natalie for gifting me a copy of this masterpiece.</i><br>You can read this review on <a href="https://bookishfever.wordpress.com/2016/09/25/the-silent-waters-elements-3-by-brittainy-c-cherry-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">BookishFever</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17159407892392711954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1760891634" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1760891634" />
    <a title="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10312276-melissa-mel-reader"><img alt="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517366723p2/10312276.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1760891634?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" href="/user/show/10312276-melissa-mel-reader">MELISSA *Mel Reader*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10312276-melissa-mel-reader?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1760891634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2044146468748499347">5+++ Love Is The Loudest Stars!<br/>(ARC provided by author)<br/>(BR with Patty & Dee)<br/><br/>-Those who believed in you when you didn't believe in yourself were the ones to hold close. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/47355C31-14FF-46CC-AA7F-2EF683E2F2AB_zpsf3zqitaq.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593977._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 47355C31-14FF-46CC-AA7F-2EF683E2F2AB_zpsf3zqitaq.jpg' width='365' height='365' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Maggie May Riley is a vibrant, happy little girl who adores her daddy. I really loved her relationship with her father. When she is six years old her father re-marries & she gains a new family she adores. They are all wonderful to her & she lives in a big home in Wisconsin near Harper Lake where she quickly settles into her ne</span>
  <span id="freeText2044146468748499347" style="display:none">5+++ Love Is The Loudest Stars!<br>(ARC provided by author)<br>(BR with Patty &amp; Dee)<br><br>-Those who believed in you when you didn't believe in yourself were the ones to hold close. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/47355C31-14FF-46CC-AA7F-2EF683E2F2AB_zpsf3zqitaq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593977._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 47355C31-14FF-46CC-AA7F-2EF683E2F2AB_zpsf3zqitaq.jpg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maggie May Riley is a vibrant, happy little girl who adores her daddy. I really loved her relationship with her father. When she is six years old her father re-marries &amp; she gains a new family she adores. They are all wonderful to her &amp; she lives in a big home in Wisconsin near Harper Lake where she quickly settles into her new wonderful life.<br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/B83DDFC3-5BFB-4D70-954E-F10ABDE2CDF3_zpswebjtsvl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593978._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo B83DDFC3-5BFB-4D70-954E-F10ABDE2CDF3_zpswebjtsvl.jpg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One of her favorite things to do is tag along and spend time with her new stepbrother &amp; his friends. She quickly grows quite fond of Brooks Tyler Griffin who lives across the street. He's her favorite of Calvin's friends &amp; has a kindness about him she's drawn to. She decides Brooks is her forever &amp; lets him know he is the one for her. Eventually he comes around to not thinking girls are gross &amp; realizes he likes Maggie May too. They are absolutely adorable! <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/71763254-7DDB-47D9-A832-6A81BEB42430_zps9te0kneu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593980._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 71763254-7DDB-47D9-A832-6A81BEB42430_zps9te0kneu.jpg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When Maggie May is around ten years old she has an experience that changes her life. She isn't the carefree little girl full of joy anymore. She's so traumatized she loses her voice. It's like her soul, innocence &amp; youth are stolen from her. Through her darkest days Brooks is her light. The one person who always stood by her &amp; fought for her. He gave her time &amp; space and never made her feel broken. Eventually Brooks moves away to follow his dreams. He returns and later tragedy strikes his life as well. Life throws many struggles their way, but together they can survive anything. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/3193BE64-FF1F-4936-92CB-ECDB00E388DF_zpsypp5o6wn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593979._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 3193BE64-FF1F-4936-92CB-ECDB00E388DF_zpsypp5o6wn.jpg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Maggie always reminded me of music. She was my music. <br><br>-It was freeing to feel so much with someone who felt it too. It was during those moments that I felt I learned the most about her. It was in those moments that she learned the most about me. I hadn't known you could hear someone's voice so clearly in the silent moments.<br><br>-The last time I'd been kissed was by the same boy who wrapped his arms around me, who held me as if I were a promise of a dream he didn't know he had.<br><br>-I felt his soul, my body pressed against his.<br><br>-Everything about his soul lit me on fire, and I was proud to burn beside him.<br><br>-Every time he touched me, I wanted more. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/0098384C-2046-4FEA-83C5-56DC86B3F9DA_zpsq5g6d0jg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593981._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0098384C-2046-4FEA-83C5-56DC86B3F9DA_zpsq5g6d0jg.jpg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I would give this book ten stars if I could. It's one of those books that will stay on my mind for a while. I adored Brooks so much! He had my heart from the moment with the night light. I was gone for him after that. Brooks simply is Maggie's joy. He's everything good &amp; pure in her life, and the one constant she can always count on. I loved how music &amp; books were so much a part of this story, &amp; we're almost like therapy. <br><br>Every time I finish a Brittainy Cherry book my heart is overflowing with emotion. No author has ever made me feel so much reading a book the way Brittainy does. Her words are beauty, truth, wisdom and love all woven together to create an unforgettable story that touches you heart &amp; soul. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/59A81724-5CD8-4FA3-ADA8-DE9170624D47_zpshk0w1xbm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474396543i/20593982._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 59A81724-5CD8-4FA3-ADA8-DE9170624D47_zpshk0w1xbm.jpg" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-The thing about love. It didn't leave because you told it to go.<br><br>-Being in love with someone didn't mean you only loved them during the sunbeams. It meant you stood by their side during the cloudy nights, too.<br><br>-She was right about me, and her, and us. She'd be the one girl I'd love until forever. No matter how life tried to change us.<br><br>-I wanted to make her smile. If I could only do one thing for the rest of my life, it would be to make her smile, and it was time for her to know that, to know how I felt.<br><br>-I've had many moments in my lifetime, moments that changed me, challenged me, moments that scared me and engulfed me. However, the biggest ones- the most heartbreaking and breathtaking ones- all included her. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/7f2a0674-9457-4206-a18b-ab26ca446dbc_zpslrutmwsc.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452003067i/17631979.png" alt=" photo 7f2a0674-9457-4206-a18b-ab26ca446dbc_zpslrutmwsc.png" width="365" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2044146468748499347" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vmFiuOIWoVCpFR1bdiS3ZRCeV7k8QUJ7UBRTkY20kek2qu6QFwQ9eSB2TkMiEHZkhp3MyxRGzdMhd3PEXO3OAA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7Hz/crT+iwLYiMb13zvGey82FfoKdUuzsWKt5See2U1kt3NaQewXK1Hrle2LDwd6uTWOiCJyxBvAAY2w9seGpA==')})
  }
